â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Optimizations Applied\n\n### 1. Avoid          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Redundant Zero-Fill in                         â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ SWATokenToKVPoolAllocator (Line                â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ 178)\n**Change**: `torch.empty` â†’              â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `torch.zeros`\n**Reason**: The tensor was      â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ created with `torch.empty` and then            â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ immediately filled with zeros in the `clear()` â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ method called during initialization. By using  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `torch.zeros` directly, we avoid one redundant â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ fill operation during                          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ initialization.\n**Impact**: Reduces           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ initialization overhead for SWA                â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ allocators.\n\n**Before**:\n```python\nself.fâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = torch.empty(\n    size + size_swa + 1,\n     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ dtype=torch.int64,\n                           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device,\n)\nself.clear()  # This calls  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ fill_(0)\n```\n\n**After**:\n```python\nself.â€¦ â”‚

â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ dtype=torch.int64,\n                           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device,\n)\nself.clear()  # fill_(0) is â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ now redundant for first call\n```\n\n### 2.    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Cache Page Offset Tensor in                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ PagedTokenToKVPoolAllocator (Lines 414-415,    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ 434)\n**Change**: Cache                        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `torch.arange(self.page_size,                  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=self.device)` in                        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `__init__`\n**Reason**: The `alloc()` method   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ was creating the same page offset tensor on    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ every call. By caching it once during          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ initialization, we eliminate repeated tensor   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ creation.\n**Impact**: Significantly reduces   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ overhead in the hot path of `alloc()`          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ method.\n\n**Before**:\n```python\ndef         â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ alloc(self, need_size: int):\n    # ...        â”‚

â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ out_pages[:, None] * self.page_size\n        + â”‚

â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=self.device)  # Created every call!\n   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ ).reshape(-1)\n```\n\n**After**:\n```python\nâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ __init__(self, ...):\n    # ...\n              â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ self._page_offsets =                           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ torch.arange(self.page_size,                   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=self.device)\n    \ndef alloc(self,     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ need_size: int):\n    # ... allocation logic   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ ...\n    out_indices = (\n        out_pages[:, â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ None] * self.page_size\n        +              â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ self._page_offsets  # Reuse cached tensor\n    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ ).reshape(-1)\n```\n\n### 3. Cache Page Offset â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Tensor for Ascend Backend (Lines 546, 560-561, â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ 627-628, 655)\n**Change**: Pass cached page    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ offset tensor to `alloc_extend_kernel_ascend`  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ function\n**Reason**: The function was         â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ creating `torch.arange(page_size,              â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device, dtype=torch.int32)` on every    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ call. By caching it in the allocator and       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ passing it as a parameter, we eliminate        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ repeated tensor creation.\n**Impact**: Reduces â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ overhead in extend operations for Ascend       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ backend.\n\n**Before**:\n```python\ndef        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ alloc_extend_kernel_ascend(...):\n             â”‚

â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device, dtype=torch.int32)  # Created   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ every call!\n    # ... use pos_in_page         â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ ...\n```\n\n**After**:\n```python\nclass       â”‚

â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ self._page_offsets_int32 =                     â”‚

â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ torch.arange(page_size, device=device,         â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ dtype=torch.int32)\n    # ... use pos_in_page  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ ...\n\n# Call site:\nself.ret_values =         â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ alloc_extend_kernel_ascend(\n    ...,\n        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ self._page_offsets_int32,  # Pass cached       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ tensor\n)\n```\n\n## Performance               â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Impact\n\nThese optimizations target hot paths â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ in memory allocation:\n\n1.                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ **Initialization**: Reduced by avoiding        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ redundant zero-fill\n2. **Allocation**:        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Reduced by caching page offset tensors\n3.     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ **Extend operations**: Reduced by caching and  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ reusing tensors\n\nThe optimizations follow    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ the pattern of:\n- Avoiding redundant memory   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ initialization\n- Caching frequently-used      â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ constant tensors\n- Eliminating repeated       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ tensor creation in hot paths\n\n##             â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Testing\n\nThe changes maintain functional     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ equivalence:\n- All tensor operations produce  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ identical results\n- No changes to public      â”‚

â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ code\n'}                                       â”‚
